---
title: "CockroachDB Downloads Archive"
old_description: "Archive of downloads for versions of CockroachDB that are no longer supported"
---

<Warning>
This page hosts download links to CockroachDB versions that are no longer supported. For more information about CockroachDB version support, refer to [Release Support Policy](/docs/releases/release-support-policy#unsupported-versions). To download and learn about currently supported CockroachDB versions, refer to [CockroachDB Releases](/docs/releases).
</Warning>

## Downloads

### v25.3

CockroachDB v25.3 is completely unsupported. This was an Innovation release that reached end-of-support on 2026-02-04.

<Tabs>

### v25.1

CockroachDB v25.1 is completely unsupported. This was an Innovation release that reached end-of-support on 2025-08-18.

### v24.2

CockroachDB v24.2 is completely unsupported. This was an Innovation release that reached end-of-support on 2025-02-12.

### v24.1

CockroachDB v24.1 is partially supported. Pre-LTS patches (before 24.1.6) are no longer supported, but LTS patches (24.1.6 and later) are still covered under the LTS support policy until 2026-10-21.

<Tab title="Windows">

#### Production Releases

Windows 8 or higher is required. Windows downloads are **experimental**. Experimental downloads are not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.

#### Production Releases

Docker images for CockroachDB are published on [Docker Hub](https://hub.docker.com/r/cockroachdb/cockroach/tags).

All Docker images for v24.1 are [Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) with support for both Intel and ARM.

</Tabs>

### v23.2

CockroachDB v23.2 is partially supported. Pre-LTS patches (before 23.2.7) are no longer supported, but LTS patches (23.2.7 and later) are still covered under the LTS support policy until 2026-07-08.

### v23.1

CockroachDB v23.1 is completely unsupported. This was a Regular release that reached end-of-support on 2024-11-15.

<Tab title="Windows">

#### Production Releases

Windows 8 or higher is required. Windows downloads are **experimental**. Experimental downloads are not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.

#### Testing Releases

Windows 8 or higher is required. Windows downloads are **experimental**. Experimental downloads are not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.

### v22.2

CockroachDB v22.2 is completely unsupported. This was a Regular release that reached end-of-support on 2024-06-05.

<Tab title="Docker">

#### Production Releases

Docker images for CockroachDB are published on [Docker Hub](https://hub.docker.com/r/cockroachdb/cockroach/tags).

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM.

### v22.1

CockroachDB v22.1 is completely unsupported. This was a Regular release that reached end-of-support on 2023-11-24.

### v21.2

CockroachDB v21.2 is completely unsupported. This was a Regular release that reached end-of-support on 2023-05-16.

### v21.1

CockroachDB v21.1 is completely unsupported. This was a Regular release that reached end-of-support on 2022-11-18.

### v20.2

CockroachDB v20.2 is completely unsupported. This was a Regular release that reached end-of-support on 2022-05-10.

### v2.1

CockroachDB v2.1 is completely unsupported. This was a Regular release that reached end-of-support on 2020-04-30.

<Tab title="Docker">

#### Production Releases

Docker images for CockroachDB are published on [Docker Hub](https://hub.docker.com/r/cockroachdb/cockroach/tags).

All Docker images for v2.1 are [Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) with support for both Intel and ARM.

<Tab title="Source">

#### Production Releases

The source code for CockroachDB is hosted in the [cockroachdb/cockroach](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases) repository on Github.

### v2.0

CockroachDB v2.0 is completely unsupported. This was a Regular release that reached end-of-support on 2019-10-04.

### v1.1

CockroachDB v1.1 is completely unsupported. This was a Regular release that reached end-of-support on 2019-04-12.

### v1.0

CockroachDB v1.0 is completely unsupported. This was a Regular release that reached end-of-support on 2018-11-10.

<Tab title="Docker">

#### Production Releases

Docker images for CockroachDB are published on [Docker Hub](https://hub.docker.com/r/cockroachdb/cockroach/tags).

All Docker images for v1.0 are [Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) with support for both Intel and ARM.
